########################################################
# Expand Aalborg Airport
########################################################
event = {
	id = 1000000
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = { control = { province = 218 data = -3 }
	}
	
	decision_trigger = { metal = 200 energy = 200 supplies = 250 }
	
	trigger = { 
		control = { province = 218 data = -3 }
	}

	name = "EVT_1000000_NAME" 
	desc = "EVT_1000000_DESC"
	style = 2
	picture = "aalborg"
	decision_picture = "aalborg_dec"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1938 }
	offset = 10
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1947 } 

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_1000000a"
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = construct which = air_base where = 218 value = 6 }
		command = { type = metalpool value = -200 }
		command = { type = energypool value = -200 }
		command = { type = supplies value = -250 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTION_NAME_NO_NEED"
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { }
	}
}

	offset = 1

	style = 2

	decision_picture = "luftlande"

		name = "ACTION_NAME_GOOD"
		command = { type = remove_division which = 14500 value = 1044 }	
		command = { type = activate_division which = 14500 value = 1045 when = 0 }																						
		command = { type = supplies value = -800 }
		command = { type = manpowerpool value = -9 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 1000435
	random = no
	country = GER

	trigger = { 
		control = { province = 338 data = GER } # Belgrade
		NOT = { exists = YUG } 
		NOT = { exists = SER } 
		NOT = { exists = CRO } 
	}

	name = "EVT_NAME_1000435"
	desc = "EVT_DESC_1000435"
	style = 2
	picture = "occupation_balkans"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1933 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action = {
		ai_chance = 0
		name = "1000435a" # Conquer
		command = { type = dissent value = 6 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 353 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 344 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 354 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 355 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 340 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 342 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 338 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 327 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 330 value = 50 }
		command = { type = province_revoltrisk which = 339 value = 50 }
	}
	action = {
		ai_chance = 100
		name = "1000435b" # Setup puppets
		command = { trigger = { ai = GER } type = activate_division which = 14500 value = 2104 where = 343 when = 0 } #Activate GAR division to help AI defend beaches
		command = { type = independence which = CRO value = 1 }
		command = { type = independence which = SER value = 1 }
		command = { type = make_puppet which = CRO }
		command = { type = make_puppet which = SER }
	}
}

	id = 1000503

	country = SOV

			AND = { 
				event = 1000502 #Stalin's evacuation event has fired

			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { event = 1000502 } #Stalin's evacuation has not fired

event = {
	id = 1000508
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = {
		exists = JAP
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = JAP } }
		event = 2003047 # German 1940 diplomatic offensive
		control = { province = 1552 data = JAP } # Tokyo
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = JAP } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = SOV country = JAP } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = ENG country = JAP } }
		control = { province = 163 data = -3 } # Berlin
		control = { province = 55 data = -3 }  # Paris
		control = { province = 617 data = -3 } # Kiev
		control = { province = 316 data = -3 } # Bucharest
		control = { province = 321 data = -3 } # Sofia
		control = { province = 377 data = -3 } # Athenes		
		control = { province = 641 data = -3 } # Sebastopol
		NOT = { event = 2011018 } #Event "Fading Sun" (defeat vs. China) has NOT fired
		NOT = { event = 2011028 } #Japan has not lost vs. USSR or USA
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
		war = { country = GER country = SOV }
		NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = CHI } } 
		control = { province = 572 data = -3 } # Moscow 		#Operation Typhoon was successful, hypothetical requirement for Japan to assist Germany
		OR = {
			control = { province = 663 data = -3 } # Stalingrad
			control = { province = 553 data = -3 } # Leningrad
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		exists = JAP
		event = 2003047 # German 1940 diplomatic offensive
		war = { country = GER country = SOV }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = JAP } }
		NOT = { war = { country = JAP country = CHI } }		
		NOT = { alliance = { country = GER country = JAP } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = SOV country = JAP } }
		NOT = { alliance = { country = ENG country = JAP } }
		control = { province = 163 data = -3 } # Berlin
		control = { province = 55 data = -3 }  # Paris

		control = { province = 316 data = -3 } # Bucharest

		control = { province = 663 data = -3 } # Stalingrad
		control = { province = 163 data = -3 } # Berlin

		control = { province = 663 data = -3 } # Stalingrad
		control = { province = 553 data = -3 } # Leningrad
		}

		NOT = { event = 2011018 } #Event "Fading Sun" (defeat vs. China) has NOT fired

##############################################################################
#  Operation Gertrude
##############################################################################
event = { 
	id = 1000526
	random = no 
	country = GER

	decision = {
		exists = TUR
		control = { province = 55 data = -3 } # Paris
		control = { province = 232 data = -3 } # Warzaw
		control = { province = 163 data = -3 } # Berlin
		event = 2003046 #Operation Barbarossa has launched
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Italy country = -3 data = 1 }
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = TUR }
			alliance = { country = GER country = TUR }
			exists = YUG
			year = 1942 #Operation Barbarossa has failed to achieve decisive victory before 1942
		}
	}
	
	decision_trigger = {
			NOT = { non_aggression = { country = GER country = TUR } } 
			region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 } #Germany or allies do NOT control Caucasus region
	}
	
	trigger = {
		exists = TUR
		control = { province = 55 data = -3 } # Paris
		control = { province = 232 data = -3 } # Warzaw
		control = { province = 163 data = -3 } # Berlin
		event = 2003046 #Operation Barbarossa has launched
		region = { region = Germany country = -3 data = 1 } 
		region = { region = Benelux country = -3 data = 1 }
		region = { region = Italy country = -3 data = 1 }
		NOT = { non_aggression = { country = GER country = TUR } } 
		region = { region = Kaukasus country = -3 data = 1 } #Germany or allies do NOT control Caucasus region
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = TUR }
			alliance = { country = GER country = TUR }
			exists = YUG
			year = 1942 #Operation Barbarossa has failed to achieve decisive victory before 1942
		}
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = may year = 1940 }
	offset = 30
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_1000526_NAME" 
	desc = "EVT_1000526_DESC" 
	style = 2
	picture = "Wehrmacht"
	decision_picture = "decision_barbarossa"
	
	action = {
		name = "1000526a"
		ai_chance = 10
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
		command = { type = war which = TUR }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 409 }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1076 }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1067 }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 1063 }
		command = { type = addclaim which = 386 }
	}

################################################
# Enemy at the gate - easy/normal
################################################
event = {
	id = 1000556
	random = no
	country = SOV

	decision = {
		local_flag = Stalin_stays
		war = { country = GER country = SOV }
		control = { province = 572 data = SOV } # Moscow
		OR = {
			lost_national = { country = SOV value = 10 }
			NOT = { land_percentage = { country = GER value = 0.5 } }
		}
		OR = {
			control = { province = 567 data = GER } # Around Moscow
			control = { province = 568 data = GER }
			control = { province = 570 data = GER }
			control = { province = 571 data = GER }
			control = { province = 678 data = GER }
		}
	}
	decision_trigger = { 
		control = { province = 572 data = SOV } #Moscow
		control = { province = 668 data = SOV } #Kuybyshev
	}
	trigger = {
		local_flag = Stalin_stays
		war = { country = GER country = SOV }
		control = { province = 572 data = SOV } # Moscow
		control = { province = 668 data = SOV } #Kuybyshev
		OR = {
			lost_national = { country = SOV value = 10 }
			NOT = { land_percentage = { country = GER value = 0.5 } }
		}
		OR = {
			control = { province = 567 data = GER } # Around Moscow
			control = { province = 568 data = GER }
			control = { province = 570 data = GER }
			control = { province = 571 data = GER }
			control = { province = 678 data = GER }
		}
	}

	name = 2611name
	desc = 2611desc
	style = 2
  	picture = "news_paper"

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = 2611a
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = relation which = ENG value = 25 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SOVMoscow }
	}
	action = {
		name = 2611b
		ai_chance = 1
		command = { type = capital which = 668 } # Kubyschiev
		command = { type = relation which = ENG value = -15 }
		command = { type = construct which = infrastructure where = 572 value = -40 }
		command = { type = construct which = ic where = 572 value = -5 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 5 }
	}
}
#########################################################################
#  Sue for peace with the Germans - hard version
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 1000557
	random = no
	country = SOV

	trigger = {
		war = { country = GER country = SOV }
		NOT = { ispuppet = GER }
		random = 35
		OR = {
			AND = {
				control = { province = 55 data = -2 } # Paris is controlled by an enemy
				lost_national = { country = SOV value = 35 }
				NOT = { land_percentage = { country = GER value = 0.3 } } #SOV has not enough troops
				NOT = { lost_national = { country = GER value = 7 } } #Germany is not losing national provinces
				NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ENG } } #Germany is concentrated on the Soviet front
				NOT = {	war = { country = GER country = FRA } }
				NOT = { war = { country = GER country = USA } }
				NOT = { war = { country = GER country = ITA } }
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { control = { province = 542 data = SOV } } # Arkhangelsk
				NOT = { control = { province = 572 data = SOV } } # Moscow
				NOT = { control = { province = 553 data = SOV } } # Leningrad
				NOT = { control = { province = 644 data = SOV } } # Rostov
				NOT = { control = { province = 641 data = SOV } } # Sevastopol
				NOT = { control = { province = 663 data = SOV } } # Stalingrad
				NOT = { control = { province = 668 data = SOV } } # Kujbysev
				NOT = { control = { province = 667 data = SOV } } # Tolyatti
				NOT = { control = { province = 706 data = SOV } } # Astrakhan
				NOT = { control = { province = 713 data = SOV } } # Baku
				NOT = { lost_national = { country = GER value = 7 } } #Germany is not losing national provinces
				OR = { #one of the following must be true
					local_flag = SOVMoscow  #Stalin remained in Moscow and was captured
					NOT = { control = { province = 1151 data = SOV } } # Sverdlovsk
					NOT = { control = { province = 1191 data = SOV } } # Vladivostok
					AND = { 
						nuked = -1  #was nuked at least once
						NOT = { nuked = 1 } #SOV never launched nukes
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { nuked = 1 } #SOV never launched nukes
				lost_national = { country = SOV value = 15 } #SOV is losing ground
				nuked = { country = GER  country = SOV data = 1 where = 572 } # Moscow nuked
				OR = {
					nuked = { country = GER  country = SOV data = 8 }#SOV nuked 8 times by GER
					AND = {
						nuked = { country = GER  country = SOV data = 1 where = 553 } # Leningrad nuked
						nuked = { country = GER  country = SOV data = 1 where = 663 } # Stalingrad nuked
						nuked = { country = GER  country = SOV data = 1 where = 713 } # Baku nuked
					}
				}
			}					
		}
	}
	
	name = "EVT_2624_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_2624_DESC"
	style = 2
	picture = "news_paper"
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 10 # Check for trigger conditions every ten days
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }
	
	action = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME2624A"
		
		command = { trigger = { war = { country = ENG country = GER }} type = relation which = ENG value = -15 }
		command = { trigger = { war = { country = U01 country = GER }} type = relation which = U01 value = -15 }
		command = { trigger = { war = { country = USA country = GER }} type = relation which = USA value = -15 }
		command = { type = dissent value = 20 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 2003093 }
		command = { type = removecore which = 619 } # Mogiliv-Podil's'kij - Ukraine
		command = { type = removecore which = 620 } # Balta - Ukraine
		command = { type = removecore which = 626 } # Odesa - Ukraine
		command = { type = headofstate which = 30094 } #Georgy M. Malenkov
		command = { type = headofgovernment which = 30017 } #Beria
		command = { type = foreignminister which = 30020 } #Andrey J. Vyshinsky
		command = { type = armamentminister which = 30089 } #Georgiy K. Zhukov
		command = { type = ministerofsecurity which = 30028 } #Beria
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 30002 } #Stalin
		command = { type = sleepminister which = 30021 } #Molotov
		command = { type = trigger which = 2003077 } # GER
	}
}

	country = FIN

	trigger = { 
		war = { country = FIN country = SOV }

###### Transport training AI events (AI transports training) #######
event = {
	id = 1100950
	random = no
	TAG = { USA GER ITA JAP ENG }
	persistent = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		manpower = 125
		navy = { size = 12 type = 1 where = 1 which = 1 } #Check if we have a non-transport/non-sub navy of at least 12 ships. Don't train otherwise because they will just die
		OR = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						NOT = { transport = { country = -1 value = 24 when = 1 } }
						OR = {
						country = JAP
						country = USA
						}
					}
					AND = {
						NOT = { transport = { country = -1 value = 16 when = 1 } }
						AND = {
							NOT = { country = USA }
							NOT = { country = JAP }
							}
						}
					}
				atwar = yes
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						country = GER
						war = { country = GER country = SOV }
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { transport = { country = -1 value = 9 } }
				atwar = yes
				AND = {
					country = GER
					war = { country = GER country = SOV } #Don't want GER to get 16 TRA when atwar with SOV!
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
			lost_national = { country = -1 value = 5 }
				OR = {
				country = GER
				country = USA
				country = ITA
				}
			}
		}
	}

	name = "AI_EVENT"
	style = 0

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1940 }
	offset = 14
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action_a = {
		command = { type = build_division which = transport cost = 0.5 }
		command = { trigger = { random = 10 AND = { NOT = { light_cruiser = { country = -1 value = 10 } } } } type = build_division which = light_cruiser cost = 0.5  }
		command = { trigger = { country = USA random = 70 NOT = { destroyer = { country = -1 value = 50 } } } type = build_division which = destroyer cost = 0.5  }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { country = USA } random = 30 AND = { NOT = { destroyer = { country = -1 value = 20 } } } } type = build_division which = destroyer cost = 0.5  }
	}
}

##############Recycle Transport Planes each winter from 1941 onwards, but skip years 43 & 44. Risky to do bc it can cancel invasions but the alternative is no invasions at all once the plane gets inentiveably stuck
event = {
	id = 1100958
	random = no
	TAG = { SOV USA ENG GER U55 }
	persistent = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes #Don't bother with recycling at peace
		AND = {
			month = 10 #only after october
			NOT = { month = 11 } #not in december. We re-add planes in december
			}
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				year = 1943
				NOT = { year = 1945 }
				}
			}
		OR = {
			AND = { 	
				transport_plane = { country = -1 value = 1 } #Don't respawn when only 1 and not in cycle because that way it's just suiciding the paratrooper
				local_flag = TPlaneBool
				}
			AND = { 	
				transport_plane = { country = -1 value = 2 }
				NOT = { local_flag = TPlaneBool }
				}
		}
		paratrooper = { country = -1 value = 1 } #Don't bother doing this if we don't have any paras
		NOT = { lost_national = { country = -1 value = 5 } } #Don't bother doing this if we're losing territory
	}

	name = "AI_EVENT"
	style = 0

	date = { day = 1 month = october year = 1941 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action_a = {
		command = { type = demobilize which = transport_plane when = 0 where = 0 value = -1 } #transport plane
		command = { type = local_setflag which = TPlaneRecycle when = 1 value = 1 } #Add 1 to recycle flag. Default value is 0!, so remember that this will be be 1! after one plane
		command = { type = local_setflag which = TPlaneBool } #disable transport reinforcement events
	}
}
event = {
	id = 1100959
	random = no
	TAG = { SOV USA ENG GER U55 }
	persistent = yes

	trigger = {
		ai = yes
		atwar = yes #Don't bother with recycling at peace
		month = 11 #only in december
		local_flag = { which = TPlaneRecycle value = 1 } #TPlaneRecycle greater or equal to 1
		NOT = { transport_plane = { country = -1 value = 8 } } #Not the best solution rn but let's just not respawn over 8 =/
		NOT = { lost_national = { country = -1 value = 5 } } #Don't bother doing this if we're losing territory
	}

	name = "AI_EVENT"
	style = 0

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1940 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	action_a = {
		command = { type = build_division which = transport_plane when = 1 cost = -0.1 where = 5 } #build over add because build automatically selects the newest. Cheat w/ completion date and cost because it was already a div the AI owned
		command = { 
			trigger = { 
				NOT = { paratrooper = { country = -1 value = 5 } } 
				OR = { 
					AND = { 
						NOT = { country = GER }
						NOT = { technology = 2330 } #Glider Art
						}
					AND = { 
						country = GER
						NOT = { technology = 2050 } #Glider Armor
						NOT = { technology = 2330 } #Glider Art
						}
					}
				}
		type = build_division which = paratrooper when = 1 cost = -0.1 where = 3 } #on average, removing TPs will accidentally delete at least 1 para div. Let's make sure it's rebuilt
		command = { 
			trigger = { 
				NOT = { paratrooper = { country = -1 value = 5 } } 
				OR = { 
					AND = { 
						NOT = { country = GER }
						technology = 2330 #Glider Art
						}
					AND = { 
						country = GER
						NOT = { technology = 2050 } #Glider Armor
						technology = 2330 #Glider Art
						}
					}
				}
		type = build_division which = paratrooper value = glider_artillery when = 1 cost = -0.1 where = 3 }
		command = { 
			trigger = { 
				NOT = { paratrooper = { country = -1 value = 5 } } 
					AND = { 
						country = GER
						technology = 2050 #Glider Armor
						}
				}
		type = build_division which = paratrooper value = glider_armor when = 1 cost = -0.1 where = 3 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = TPlaneRecycle when = 1 value = -1 } #Subtract 1 from the recycle flag. Default value is 1, so remember that this will be down to 1 after respawnin one plane
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = { which = TPlaneRecycle value = 2 } } } type = local_clrflag which = TPlaneBool } #enable transport reinforcement if we're done with re-training :D
	}
}

########## GER and SOV Tank Development -
########## German Tanks are large (comfortable to use -> higher org, morale) but generally bad vs armor early on and easy to penetrate. Soviets are generally tougher but have hard to use, cramped tanks. and bad AT capabilities for Lights. Ideally write event text for this
########## Give GER some armor back in the "sloped armor" event

        random = no 
		tag = { SOV }

        }

        desc = EVT_1000554_DESC 
        style = 2

        offset = 20

				command = { type = morale which = armor value = -3 }

event = {
	id = 2003190
	random = no
	tag = { ENG }
   
	name = "EVT_NAME_21371"
	desc = "EVT_DESC_21371" 
	style = 2
	picture = "baku2"
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = USA } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = BEL } }
		NOT = { event = 1000731 } ###  The Fall of France (GER)
		NOT = { lost_national = { country = ENG value = 10 } }
		NOT = { lost_national = { country = FRA value = 10 } }
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1940 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = april year = 1940 }
	action = {
		ai_chance = 5 # 5 normally, debugging
		name = "ACTIONNAME2024B"
		command = { type = war which = SOV }
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 } #5
		command = { type = supplies value = -300 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 1 }
		command = { type = relation which = USA value = -40 }
		command = { type = relation which = SOV value = -80 }
		command = { type = end_trades which = ENG where = SOV }
		command = { type = event which = 2003191 where = SOV when = 3 }
		command = { type = event which = 2003192 where = GER when = 5 }
		command = { type = event which = 2003193 where = FRA when = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = ENG } type = ai which = "switch/ENG_Pike.ai" }
	}	
	action = { 
		ai_chance = 95 #95
		name = "ACTINUTILE"
		command = { }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 2003201
	random = no
	TAG = { AFG ARA ARG AUS AST BEL BOL BRA BUL CAL CAN CHC CHI CHL COL CSA CZE DDR DEN DFR EAF EGY ENG ETH EST FIN FLA FRA GEO GER GRE HOL HUN IDC IND INO IRE IRQ ISR ITA JAP KOR LAT LBY LIT MAN MEN MEX NOR NZL OTT PAK PAR PER POL POR PRK PRU QUE ROM RSI RUS SAF SAU SCA SCH SCO SER SIA SLO SLV SOV SPA SPR SWE TEX TUR UKR VEN VIC VIE WLL YUG USA U01 u02 u03 u08 u09 u10 u11 u12 u13 u14 u15 u16 u17 u18 u19 u20 u21 u22 u26 u27 u28 u29 u30 u31 u32 u33 u34 u35 u40 u41 u42 u43 u44 u45 u46 u47 u48 u72 u73 u74 u77 u78 } 

	trigger = { 
	ai = no
	flag = DDay
		AND = {
			OR = {
				garrison = { country = USA province = 125  type = land size = 7 area = 2 } #Rotterdam, Flanders Region

				garrison = { country = U01 province = 125  type = land size = 7 area = 2 } #Rotterdam, Flanders Region
				garrison = { country = U01 province = 43  type = land size = 5 area = 1 } #Cherbourg, Normandy Area
				garrison = { country = U01 province = 37  type = land size = 5 area = 1 } #Brest, Brittany Area

				region = { region = "France" country = USA value = 3 }
